http.NewServeMux()\n\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/evaluate/v1/boolean\", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest\n\t\tif err := protojson.New().UnmarshalOptions.Unmarshal(readBody(nil, r), &req); err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Return error response in gRPC status format\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\terrorResp := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"code\":    3, // INVALID_ARGUMENT\n\t\t\t\t\"message\": \"Invalid request body\",\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(errorResp)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresp, err := evalServer.Boolean(r.Context(), &req)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Return error response in gRPC status format\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\terrorResp := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"code\":    2, // INTERNAL\n\t\t\t\t\"message\": err.Error(),\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(errorResp)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\trespData, _ := protojson.Marshal(resp)\n\t\tw.Write(respData)\n\t})\n\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/evaluate/v1/variant\", func(w http.NewServeMux()\n\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/evaluate/v1/boolean\", func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\tif r.Method != http.MethodPost {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Method not allowed\", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar req rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest\n\t\tif err := protojson.Unmarshal(readBodyFromRequest(nil, r), &req); err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Return error response in gRPC status format\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusBadRequest)\n\t\t\terrorResp := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"code\":    3, // INVALID_ARGUMENT\n\t\t\t\t\"message\": \"Invalid request body\",\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(errorResp)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tresp, err := evalServer.Boolean(r.Context(), &req)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// Return error response in gRPC status format\n\t\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\terrorResp := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"code\":    2, // INTERNAL\n\t\t\t\t\"message\": err.Error(),\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(errorResp)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"application/json\")\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\t\trespData, _ := protojson.Marshal(resp)\n\t\tw.Write(respData)\n\t})\n\n\tmux.HandleFunc(\"/evaluate/v1/variant\", func(w
